class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-d54a3bd1-0 gHLXBH iIduIB"><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Sending a calendar invite is the best way to ensure everybody is on the same page for an event. From birthday parties to corporate meetings, life runs much smoother when everybody knows when and where they need to be.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">When it comes to event planning and follow-up, the days when people needed to write all the details down on their planners are long gone. Current technology allows us to skip unnecessary phone calls, texts, and emails to agree on times and dates. There's also no need to contact participants individually to keep them posted on plan changes. You can now reach all invitees at once in a few simple steps. The right <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/scheduling-software-companies"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">scheduling software</span></span></a></span> makes event-related communication easier than ever.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">But Calendly is <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/features"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">not your average digital calendar</span></span></a></span>. It's a simple yet powerful tool that helps you save time in your workflow managing calendar invites, as well as event update notifications and text reminders. But you don't need to be a top-floor executive to use this scheduling automation. Calendly makes event planning accessible for everyone.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Entrepreneurs, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/solutions/sales"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">sales reps</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/solutions/recruiting"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">recruiters</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/solutions/education"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">educators</span></span></a></span>… anyone can take advantage of Calendly. You can use it to spread the word about social events, meetings, appointments, conference calls, online classes, or any other event you have. The platform lets you share two kinds of links to make this task way easier:</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Sharing a link to your <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/360038853154" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">main scheduling page</span></span></a></span> lets people see your overall availability and find the right time to book a meeting with you. It gives attendees access to your landing page, where they can see all the types of events you offer.&nbsp;</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Sharing an event-specific link is more personal. It provides information on one particular type of event only (for example, a 30-minute video chat). </p></li></ul><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">To send your Calendly event link, follow these simple steps:</p><h3 id="Step-1:-Create-a-unique-Event-Type-and-Calendly-link" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Step 1: Create a unique Event Type and Calendly link</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly lets you create different types of events. This tool helps you keep your schedule organized, narrow down the information you share, and target the right audience for each invite.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly automatically generates a unique URL for each new event you create. You can <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/360038853154" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">customize and share</span></span></a></span> these URLs for extra personalization. Your Calendly link is a shareable shortcut to all the necessary information about your event. It contains locations, durations, starting times, dates, and more.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly also allows you to create single-use links to <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/223193448-Sharing-your-scheduling-link#control-who-schedules-with-you-0-5" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">limit access to a specific Event Type</span></span></a></span>. The URL becomes invalid once your invitee uses it to schedule the event. To create a single-use link:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to your Calendly home page</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to<span font-style="italic" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 jEIfWj"> </span>“Event type"</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Locate the event you want to share</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Select “Share” on the event tile</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Click on “Let this link expire after the first booking”</p></li></ol><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="KB Single-use link" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="KB Single-use link" loading="lazy" width="1508" height="1148" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/6ypAGDxuZv7LNLUX3dJCqYasset/4bd9dd69cab86dd9f42575da42361aae/KB_Single-use_link_19APR2021.jpeg?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly offers several other choices to manage your schedule and create your events. You can take advantage of these and other features by using the<span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/115002214194" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"> <span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Chrome</span></span></a></span> and<span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://help.calendly.com/hc/en-us/articles/360035393573" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"> <span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Firefox extensions</span></span></a></span> or the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.calendly.app&amp;hl=en_US&amp;gl=US" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Android</span></span></a></span> and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/calendly-mobile/id1451094657" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">iPhone</span></span></a></span> apps.&nbsp;</p><h3 id="Step-2:-Locate-your-Event-Type's-unique-Calendly-link" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Step 2: Locate your Event Type's unique Calendly link</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">To find the Calendly link for a particular event, all you need to do is:&nbsp;</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Access your<span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="/app/login" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"> <span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly account</span></span></a></span></p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to the home page</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to “Event type”</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Select the event you want to share</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Click on “Copy link”</p></li></ol><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Image showing where to copy the scheduling link for an Event Type in Calendly" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Image showing where to copy the scheduling link for an Event Type in Calendly" loading="lazy" width="656" height="574" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/5KginHmgYHXjdBtyr0MNfhasset/66689b7eb430c9bba9d35d6418087179/20_minute_call_Event_Type_example.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></figure><h3 id="Step-3:-Find-the-best-channel-to-share-your-calendar-invite" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Step 3: Find the best channel to share your calendar invite</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Before going further, it’s important to get agreement on the time, date, and location for your meeting. (<b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">Pro tip: </b>Use the <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/blog/meeting-polls"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Meeting Polls</span></span></a></span> feature to let your invitees vote on what available times work best.) Then you can confirm your meeting by sending your Calendly link. Most people go for the classic email to get on invitee schedules, but there are alternatives.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If it's more comfortable for everyone involved, you can use social media, direct messaging apps, or co-working tools like <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH" href="/integration/slack"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Slack</span></span></a></span> to share your scheduled event. Once you decide on the proper channel to share your invite, all you have to do is copy/paste your Calendly link. No more back-and-forth scheduling messages!</p><h3 id="Step-4:-Craft-an-engaging-and-clear-message-to-your-invitees" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Step 4: Craft an engaging and clear message to your invitees</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Regardless of the importance of the event, you should make your meeting invite feel personal and welcoming. Sending your link by itself doesn’t give that impression — or get good response rates. Recipients can easily overlook a calendar invite without a clear introduction.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Avoid the problem by crafting a straightforward message. It can be something as simple as, “Here's the calendar invite link [anchor Calendly link] for our meeting so we can all be on the same page.”</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Need some more inspiration? Here are a few short templates you can use for different scenarios. Read them carefully and pick the right one to communicate with all attendees effectively.‌</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">‌Sales call‌ follow-up</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“Thank you for your interest in our [insert product or service]. Let's talk more about your expectations and how we can help you meet them. Click here [anchor Calendly link] to see all the information about the call we scheduled earlier today.”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Social event</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“I'm so excited to celebrate my [insert Event Type] with you. Click here [anchor Calendly link] to find all you need to know about the event. We'll have a wonderful time. Can't wait to see you there!”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Webinar/online course</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“Thank you for signing up for our [insert event-specific information]. Click here [anchor Calendly link] to review the time and date of the event. Please reach out with any questions. See you soon!”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Client check-in call‌</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“We hope you're enjoying your new [insert product or service]. How is everything going? We'd like to schedule a call to answer any questions you may have. Click here [anchor Calendly link] for more information.‌”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Medical appointment</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“Thanks for confirming your appointment with [insert practitioner's name]. In this link [anchor Calendly link], you’ll find all the information you need for your next visit. See you then!”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Advising appointment‌</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“Thanks for scheduling a meeting to discuss your academic progress. Here's our scheduling link [anchor Calendly link] with the hours and location we agreed on for your appointment. Please reach out with any further questions.”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Job interview</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“At [insert company's name], we're impressed with your resume and skillset. We’re very excited to get to know you and see if we're a perfect match. Click here [anchor Calendly link] for scheduling details for your interview. We can't wait to meet you!”</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">‌General networking‌</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">“I'm looking forward to discussing more ideas with you. Here's our scheduling link [anchor Calendly link] to avoid the back and forth with our meeting's date, time, and location. See you soon!‌”</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">You can always add your full link below your message for your invitees to copy/paste it on their browsers. However, your invite looks a lot cleaner if you use<span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.businessinsider.com/guides/tech/how-to-create-a-hyperlink-in-outlook" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dMOOdH"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"> <span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">clickable hyperlinked text</span></span></a></span>. Some email platforms such as Microsoft Outlook and Gmail have a built-in tool to make hyperlinks. If you're sending your invite via text message or social media, you probably won't be able to generate a hyperlink. In these scenarios, it's okay to keep it simple and simply copy/paste the URL.&nbsp;</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-switchback" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 iiTDiY"><div overflow="hidden" data-testid="callout-switchback-image" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 cqdiqK"><div width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 kvHEiz bTbbHj next-image-wrapper" display="flex"><img alt="E-book: Scheduling etiquette" loading="lazy" width="0" height="0" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/4816uqFH5Wa9Hm1Sao3ByL/173a7c2dfd747f7443eaf4a578393144/-E-book-_Making_scheduling_human__The_Calendly_guide_to_etiquette.png?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></div><div direction="column" width="100%" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 dhjnTZ"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 bhbaoe"><h4 data-testid="callout-switchback-title" font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 jafAqy">E-book: Scheduling etiquette</h4></div><div data-testid="callout-switchback-body" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 sc-eaa94a81-0 eFMMXe bDJlSh">Are scheduling links rude? Depends on how you share them! Download this e-book for advice on sharing your calendar link politely.<div class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-9f52a7fd-5 kXCqii beZgaB button-container" width="100%" display="flex"><a data-testid="primary-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 dCoJlx" href="/resources/ebooks/scheduling-etiquette"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx">Get your copy</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="‌Step-5:-Share-your-Calendly-link" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">‌Step 5: Share your Calendly link</h3><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Once your invite has all the necessary details, you can finally send it to your invitees. Calendly's event shareability helps you spread the word to the right people from your computer or mobile device.&nbsp;</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Send a Calendly calendar invite from a web browser</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If you're using your computer, follow these instructions to share your Calendly event link:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Access your Calendly account</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Select the event you want to share</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Double-check all information is correct</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Choose the platform you're using to share your invite</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Copy your link and paste it into your message</p></li></ol><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="On your booking page, hit &quot;copy link&quot; to grab the scheduling link for a particular event type." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="On your booking page, hit &quot;copy link&quot; to grab the scheduling link for a particular event type." loading="lazy" width="2036" height="674" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/4g4zHgiY3lhgjENalatJBdasset/f01e8c8ed5a52245c635cf5a3c1a57fd/KB_Share_link_to_booking_page_19APR2021.jpg?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></figure><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Emailing has always been a fantastic option to reach multiple people at once. Other apps and sites also let you connect with numerous people from your contact list at the same time. No matter what platform you're using, make sure all interested parties appear in your recipient field before you hit “send.”&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Once your guests have the link, they'll be able to further spread the word by resending the invite to others. If you prefer they don't share the scheduling link elsewhere, make sure to send a single-use link.&nbsp;</p><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Send a Calendly calendar invite from a browser extension</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Download the Calendly extension on Google Chrome or Mozilla Firefox, then:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Click on the Calendly icon on your browser's toolbar</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Locate the event you want to share</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Use the dropdown arrow to display the options</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Select “Copy link”</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Paste the link into your message‌</p></li></ol><figure direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcNCVO"><div data-testid="image" title="Calendly's Chrome extension lets you easily copy your scheduling link to paste into an email." class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-bf28344b-0 bhbaoe ezMOoT next-image-wrapper" display="flex" width="100%"><img data-testid="image" alt="Calendly's Chrome extension lets you easily copy your scheduling link to paste into an email." loading="lazy" width="600" height="431" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" style="color:transparent;object-fit:contain" src="https://images.ctfassets.net/k0lk9kiuza3o/1eKgxoiMm3vl1tg2WKeh97asset/a3ae45cba0cfd910b54bf42569def34b/sidebar.gif?q=85&amp;fm=webp"></div></figure><h4 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 fWbnVd">Send a Calendly calendar invite from Android or iPhone</h4><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">On your smartphone, you may choose to share your link via email or text message. If you're using Calendly on Android or iPhone, your app will automatically compose a default message for you to share with your invitees. You can always edit our pre-written message. All you have to do is:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to your Event Types screen</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Tap on the menu icon</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Select “Default message”</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Modify the text to your preference</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Tap <b font-weight="bold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 gfdHMB">“</b>Save”</p></li></ol><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">‌Once you're happy with the message, you can share your link:</p><ol class="sc-9f52a7fd-2 kxVxVi"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Go to the Event Types screen</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Find the event you want to share</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Tap “Share”</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Choose the method to share the link. You can pick:&nbsp;</p><ul class="sc-9f52a7fd-1 buUria"><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Send email</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Sent text</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Copy link</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Create QR</p></li><li><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">More options&nbsp;</p></li></ul></li></ol><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">If you select email or text, Calendly will launch the chosen app and display your message and link. All you'll have to do next is add your desired recipients and send. Alternatively, you can add the link to your clipboard by selecting "Copy link" and manually pasting it into your preferred platform. Finally, you can pick "More options," and Calendly will display other apps that might allow you to share your link.</p><h2 id="Ready-to-start-sharing?" class="sc-372af2a2-0 dqpylw">Ready to start sharing?</h2><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">When you're planning any event, there's nothing more frustrating than not getting your message to everyone involved. Calendly lets you optimize your time and send your calendar invites faster and more effectively. Once you share your link, the planning process becomes a lot less stressful.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Whether you've already decided the time, date, and location of your event, or you're still figuring it all out, this powerful scheduling software lets you focus on the important details. Forget about the back-and-forth and say hello to more efficient communication.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%"
